19:T1a473,## B. Mon2tr

### Problem Description

**请注意本题特殊的空间限制。**

*"生命野蛮蓬勃，大地千变万化。人造机器轰鸣运作，源石能的光辉照亮了暗影。人们挣扎在暗处，向往光明，在辉煌时轻视阴影，如是反复。"*

给定一棵由编号为 [[$1,2,3,\cdots,n$][[[]{.strut
style="height: 0.8389em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"}[1]{.mord}[,]{.mpunct}[]{.mspace
style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"}[2]{.mord}[,]{.mpunct}[]{.mspace

style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"}[n]{.mord
.mathnormal}]{.base}]{.katex-html aria-hidden="true"}]
的点构成的有根树。记 [[$d_{i}$][[[]{.strut
style="height: 0.8444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"}[[d]{.mord
.mathnormal}[[[[[[]{.pstrut style="height: 2.7em;"}[[i]{.mord

style="height: 0.15em;"}]{.vlist-r}]{.vlist-t
.vlist-t2}]{.msupsub}]{.mord}]{.base}]{.katex-html
aria-hidden="true"}] 表示编号为 [[$i$][[[]{.strut
style="height: 0.6595em;"}[i]{.mord .mathnormal}]{.base}]{.katex-html
aria-hidden="true"}]（[[$1 \leq i \leq n$][[[]{.strut
style="height: 0.7804em; vertical-align: -0.136em;"}[1]{.mord}[]{.mspace
style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}[≤]{.mrel}[]{.mspace

**点数**（对于树根本身，这个值为 [[$1$][[[]{.strut

[[$x_{i},y_{i},z_{i}$][[[]{.strut

    aria-hidden="true"}] 表示取模，例如
    [[$3\operatorname{}2 = 1,( - 7)\operatorname{}3 = 2$][[[]{.strut

    style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}[=]{.mrel}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
    style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"}[1]{.mord}[,]{.mpunct}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"}[(]{.mopen}[−]{.mord}[7]{.mord}[)]{.mclose}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.0556em;"}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"}[[[mod]{.mord
    .mathrm}]{.mord}]{.mbin}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.0556em;"}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
    style="height: 0.6444em;"}[3]{.mord}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}[=]{.mrel}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
    style="height: 0.6444em;"}[2]{.mord}]{.base}]{.katex-html
    aria-hidden="true"}]。

保证输入的是一棵有根树。

### Output

对于每一组测试数据，输出包含 [[$q$][[[]{.strut
style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"}[q]{.mord
.mathnormal style="margin-right: 0.0359em;"}]{.base}]{.katex-html
aria-hidden="true"}] 行。

第 [[$i$][[[]{.strut style="height: 0.6595em;"}[i]{.mord
.mathnormal}]{.base}]{.katex-html
aria-hidden="true"}]（[[$1 \leq i \leq q$][[[]{.strut
style="height: 0.7804em; vertical-align: -0.136em;"}[1]{.mord}[]{.mspace
style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}[≤]{.mrel}[]{.mspace
style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
style="height: 0.7955em; vertical-align: -0.136em;"}[i]{.mord
.mathnormal}[]{.mspace
style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}[≤]{.mrel}[]{.mspace
style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"}[q]{.mord
.mathnormal style="margin-right: 0.0359em;"}]{.base}]{.katex-html
aria-hidden="true"}]）行包含一个整数表示第
[[$i$][[[]{.strut style="height: 0.6595em;"}[i]{.mord
.mathnormal}]{.base}]{.katex-html aria-hidden="true"}]
次询问的答案。

1a:T4fd63,
<h2>B. Mon2tr</h2>
<h3>Problem Description</h3>
<p><strong>请注意本题特殊的空间限制。</strong></p>
<p><em>"生命野蛮蓬勃，大地千变万化。人造机器轰鸣运作，源石能的光辉照亮了暗影。人们挣扎在暗处，向往光明，在辉煌时轻视阴影，如是反复。"</em></p>
<p>
  给定一棵由编号为 [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
        <semantics>
          <mrow>

        </semantics>
      </math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8389em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">3</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="minner">⋯</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span></span></span></span>][[[]{.strut
  style="height: 0.8389em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"}[1]{.mord}[,]{.mpunct}[]{.mspace
  style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"}[2]{.mord}[,]{.mpunct}[]{.mspace
  style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"}[3]{.mord}[,]{.mpunct}[]{.mspace

  .mathnormal}]{.base}]{.katex-html aria-hidden="true"}]
  的点构成的有根树。记 [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<p>
  现在有 [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

  style="height: 0.6595em;"}[i]{.mord .mathnormal}]{.base}]{.katex-html
  aria-hidden="true"}]（[[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

      </math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7804em;vertical-align:-0.136em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7955em;vertical-align:-0.136em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.625em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span>][[[]{.strut

<p>
  对于第 [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

  aria-hidden="true"}]（[[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

  style="height: 0.7804em; vertical-align: -0.136em;"}[1]{.mord}[]{.mspace
  style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}[≤]{.mrel}[]{.mspace

  [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3>Input</h3>

<p><strong>来自 Kal'tsit
的温馨提示：本题输入输出量较大，请使用合适的输入输出方式。你可以使用下面链接中给出的输入输出模板。同时请选手注意代码的时间和空间常数消耗，常数过大，例如滥用
C++ STL 容器的代码不保证能够通过。</strong></p>

  次询问的参数有关的三个数。

<p>
  对于第 [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

  aria-hidden="true"}]（[[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

  style="height: 0.7804em; vertical-align: -0.136em;"}[1]{.mord}[]{.mspace
  style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}[≤]{.mrel}[]{.mspace
  style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
  style="height: 0.7955em; vertical-align: -0.136em;"}[i]{.mord
  .mathnormal}[]{.mspace

  .mathnormal style="margin-right: 0.0359em;"}]{.base}]{.katex-html

    .mathnormal}[]{.mspace

    [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
          <semantics>
            <mrow>

              <mo>⁡</mo>
            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\operatorname{}</annotation>
          </semantics>
        </math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0em;"></span><span class="mop"></span></span></span></span>][[[]{.strut
    style="height: 0.6944em;"}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.0556em;"}[[[mod]{.mord
    .mathrm}]{.mord}]{.mord}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.0556em;"}]{.base}]{.katex-html
    aria-hidden="true"}] 表示取模，例如
    [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
          <semantics>
            <mrow>
              <mn>3</mn>
              <mi mathvariant="normal"></mi>
              <mo>⁡</mo>
              <mn>2</mn>
              <mo>=</mo>
              <mn>1</mn>
              <mo separator="true">,</mo>
              <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
              <mo>−</mo>
              <mn>7</mn>
              <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
              <mi mathvariant="normal"></mi>
              <mo>⁡</mo>
              <mn>3</mn>
              <mo>=</mo>
              <mn>2</mn>
            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">3\operatorname{}2 = 1,( - 7)\operatorname{}3 = 2</annotation>
          </semantics>
        </math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">3</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mop"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord">7</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mop"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">3</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span></span></span></span>][[[]{.strut
    style="height: 0.6944em;"}[3]{.mord}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.0556em;"}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"}[[[mod]{.mord
    .mathrm}]{.mord}]{.mbin}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.0556em;"}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
    style="height: 0.6444em;"}[2]{.mord}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}[=]{.mrel}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
    style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"}[1]{.mord}[,]{.mpunct}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"}[(]{.mopen}[−]{.mord}[7]{.mord}[)]{.mclose}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.0556em;"}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"}[[[mod]{.mord
    .mathrm}]{.mord}]{.mbin}[]{.mspace

    style="height: 0.6444em;"}[2]{.mord}]{.base}]{.katex-html
    aria-hidden="true"}]。
  </li>
</ol>
<p>保证输入的是一棵有根树。</p>
<h3>Output</h3>
<p>
  对于每一组测试数据，输出包含 [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
        <semantics>
          <mrow>
            <mi>q</mi>
          </mrow>
          <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q</annotation>
        </semantics>
      </math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.625em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span>][[[]{.strut
  style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"}[q]{.mord
  .mathnormal style="margin-right: 0.0359em;"}]{.base}]{.katex-html
  aria-hidden="true"}] 行。
</p>
<p>
  第 [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
        <semantics>
          <mrow>
            <mi>i</mi>
          </mrow>
          <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation>
        </semantics>
      </math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6595em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span></span></span></span>][[[]{.strut style="height: 0.6595em;"}[i]{.mord
  .mathnormal}]{.base}]{.katex-html
  aria-hidden="true"}]（[[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
        <semantics>
          <mrow>
            <mn>1</mn>
            <mo>≤</mo>
            <mi>i</mi>
            <mo>≤</mo>
            <mi>q</mi>
          </mrow>
          <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1 \leq i \leq q</annotation>
        </semantics>
      </math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7804em;vertical-align:-0.136em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7955em;vertical-align:-0.136em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.625em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span>][[[]{.strut
  style="height: 0.7804em; vertical-align: -0.136em;"}[1]{.mord}[]{.mspace
  style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}[≤]{.mrel}[]{.mspace
  style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
  style="height: 0.7955em; vertical-align: -0.136em;"}[i]{.mord
  .mathnormal}[]{.mspace
  style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}[≤]{.mrel}[]{.mspace
  style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
  style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"}[q]{.mord
  .mathnormal style="margin-right: 0.0359em;"}]{.base}]{.katex-html
  aria-hidden="true"}]）行包含一个整数表示第
  [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
        <semantics>
          <mrow>
            <mi>i</mi>
          </mrow>
          <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation>
        </semantics>
      </math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6595em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span></span></span></span>][[[]{.strut style="height: 0.6595em;"}[i]{.mord
  .mathnormal}]{.base}]{.katex-html aria-hidden="true"}]
  次询问的答案。
</p>

    .mtight}]{style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;"}]{.vlist
    style="height: 0.3117em;"}[​]{.vlist-s}]{.vlist-r}[[]{.vlist
    style="height: 0.2861em;"}]{.vlist-r}]{.vlist-t
    .vlist-t2}]{.msupsub}]{.mord}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}[=]{.mrel}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
    style="height: 0.6444em;"}[6]{.mord}]{.base}]{.katex-html
    aria-hidden="true"}]，不满足题意。
  </li>
  <li>
    若 [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
          <semantics>
            <mrow>
              <mi>j</mi>
              <mo>=</mo>
              <mn>5</mn>
            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">j = 5</annotation>
          </semantics>
        </math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.854em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">5</span></span></span></span>][[[]{.strut
    style="height: 0.854em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"}[j]{.mord
    .mathnormal style="margin-right: 0.0572em;"}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}[=]{.mrel}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
    style="height: 0.6444em;"}[5]{.mord}]{.base}]{.katex-html
    aria-hidden="true"}]，则
    [[<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
          <semantics>
            <mrow>
              <mi>j</mi>
              <mo>−</mo>
              <msub>
                <mi>v</mi>
                <mi>j</mi>
              </msub>
              <mo>=</mo>
              <mn>4</mn>
              <mo separator="true">,</mo>
              <mi>j</mi>
              <mo>+</mo>
              <msub>
                <mi>v</mi>
                <mi>j</mi>
              </msub>
              <mo>=</mo>
              <mn>6</mn>
            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">j - v_{j} = 4,j + v_{j} = 6</annotation>
          </semantics>
        </math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.854em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0359em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span     style="height: 0.854em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"}[j]{.mord
    .mathnormal style="margin-right: 0.0572em;"}[]{.mspace
    style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"}[−]{.mbin}[]{.mspace

    style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"}]{.base}[[]{.strut
    style="height: 0.854em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"}[4]{.mord}[,]{.mpunct}[]{.mspace
